Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        <h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>

        <p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

Steps to reproduce the problem:



<b class="line"><!---->Steps to reproduce the problem:<!----></b>



<br>





I'm sorry that since this function requires a chromebook and an android device to interact via Bluetooth to trigger it, I can't verify if this is a real Conditional Competition Bug.



<span class="line"><!---->I'm sorry that since this function requires a chromebook and an android device to interact via Bluetooth to trigger it, I can't verify if this is a real Conditional Competition Bug.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





If my understanding is wrong, please close this issue, thanks. :)



<span class="line"><!---->If my understanding is wrong, please close this issue, thanks. :)<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Problem Description:



<b class="line"><!---->Problem Description:<!----></b>



<br>





Android client call to BluetoothHost's BluetoothSocketConnect method via mojo.



<span class="line"><!---->Android client call to BluetoothHost's BluetoothSocketConnect method via mojo.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[



<span class="line"><!---->[<!----></span>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:ash/components/arc/mojom/bluetooth.mojom;l=484;drc=7fb345a0da63049b102e1c0bcdc8d7831110e324;bpv=1;bpt=1](https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:ash/components/arc/mojom/bluetooth.mojom;l=484;drc=7fb345a0da63049b102e1c0bcdc8d7831110e324;bpv=1;bpt=1)



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:ash/components/arc/mojom/bluetooth.mojom;l=484;drc=7fb345a0da63049b102e1c0bcdc8d7831110e324;bpv=1;bpt=1](https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:ash/components/arc/mojom/bluetooth.mojom;l=484;drc=7fb345a0da63049b102e1c0bcdc8d7831110e324;bpv=1;bpt=1)"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:ash/components/arc/mojom/bluetooth.mojom;l=484;drc=7fb345a0da63049b102e1c0bcdc8d7831110e324;bpv=1;bpt=1](https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:ash/components/arc/mojom/bluetooth.mojom;l=484;drc=7fb345a0da63049b102e1c0bcdc8d7831110e324;bpv=1;bpt=1)<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





[



<span class="line"><!---->[<!----></span>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:chrome/browser/ash/arc/bluetooth/arc_bluetooth_bridge.cc;l=3093;drc=7fb345a0da63049b102e1c0bcdc8d7831110e324;bpv=1;bpt=1](https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:chrome/browser/ash/arc/bluetooth/arc_bluetooth_bridge.cc;l=3093;drc=7fb345a0da63049b102e1c0bcdc8d7831110e324;bpv=1;bpt=1)



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:chrome/browser/ash/arc/bluetooth/arc_bluetooth_bridge.cc;l=3093;drc=7fb345a0da63049b102e1c0bcdc8d7831110e324;bpv=1;bpt=1](https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:chrome/browser/ash/arc/bluetooth/arc_bluetooth_bridge.cc;l=3093;drc=7fb345a0da63049b102e1c0bcdc8d7831110e324;bpv=1;bpt=1)"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:chrome/browser/ash/arc/bluetooth/arc_bluetooth_bridge.cc;l=3093;drc=7fb345a0da63049b102e1c0bcdc8d7831110e324;bpv=1;bpt=1](https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:chrome/browser/ash/arc/bluetooth/arc_bluetooth_bridge.cc;l=3093;drc=7fb345a0da63049b102e1c0bcdc8d7831110e324;bpv=1;bpt=1)<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





The normal logic of this function is this:



<span class="line"><!---->The normal logic of this function is this:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[0] Call CreateBluetoothConnectSocket to create a sock_wrapper



<span class="line"><!---->[0] Call CreateBluetoothConnectSocket to create a sock_wrapper<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[1] After creating the sock_wrapper, it will get its raw pointer and send OnBluetoothConnectingSocketReady to a separate thread for asynchronous execution via ThreadPool::PostTask.



<span class="line"><!---->[1] After creating the sock_wrapper, it will get its raw pointer and send OnBluetoothConnectingSocketReady to a separate thread for asynchronous execution via ThreadPool::PostTask.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[2] sock_wrapper->remote.BindNewPipeAndPassReceiver will sends the PendingReceiver to the Android client, and set sock_wrapper->remote.set_disconnect_handler, CloseBluetoothConnectingSocket method will be called when mojo is disconnected.



<span class="line"><!---->[2] sock_wrapper-&gt;remote.BindNewPipeAndPassReceiver will sends the PendingReceiver to the Android client, and set sock_wrapper-&gt;remote.set_disconnect_handler, CloseBluetoothConnectingSocket method will be called when mojo is disconnected.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[3] Transfer ownership of sock_wrapper to connecting_sockets_ via std::move



<span class="line"><!---->[3] Transfer ownership of sock_wrapper to connecting_sockets_ via std::move<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[4] OnBluetoothConnectingSocketReady running in a separate thread will be responsible for checking whether connect() is successful or not, then sock_wrapper->remote->OnConnected or OnConnected will be called. 



<span class="line"><!---->[4] OnBluetoothConnectingSocketReady running in a separate thread will be responsible for checking whether connect() is successful or not, then sock_wrapper-&gt;remote-&gt;OnConnected or OnConnected will be called. <!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[5] This will callback to the Android client (RfcommConnectingSocketClient), which will then be responsible for closing this mojo connection.



<span class="line"><!---->[5] This will callback to the Android client (RfcommConnectingSocketClient), which will then be responsible for closing this mojo connection.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Then, CloseBluetoothConnectingSocket will be called and erase the sock_wrapper from the connecting_sockets_ , thus completing a normal process.



<span class="line"><!---->Then, CloseBluetoothConnectingSocket will be called and erase the sock_wrapper from the connecting_sockets_ , thus completing a normal process.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





However: 



<span class="line"><!---->However: <!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Because the Android Client can actually disconnect the mojo at any time and OnBluetoothConnectingSocketReady runs in a separate thread in the thread pool



<span class="line"><!---->Because the Android Client can actually disconnect the mojo at any time and OnBluetoothConnectingSocketReady runs in a separate thread in the thread pool<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





There is no defined order of execution between them.



<span class="line"><!---->There is no defined order of execution between them.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





**If the mojo is disconnected immediately after the Android Client gets the PendingReceiver, then CloseBluetoothConnectingSocket will possibly erase the sock_wrapper from the connecting_sockets_ before the execution of OnBluetoothConnectingSocketReady is complete.**



<span class="line"><!---->**If the mojo is disconnected immediately after the Android Client gets the PendingReceiver, then CloseBluetoothConnectingSocket will possibly erase the sock_wrapper from the connecting_sockets_ before the execution of OnBluetoothConnectingSocketReady is complete.**<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





At this time, sock_wrapper has been released, but OnBluetoothConnectingSocketReady still holds the raw pointer of sock_wrapper, and will trigger to UAF.



<span class="line"><!---->At this time, sock_wrapper has been released, but OnBluetoothConnectingSocketReady still holds the raw pointer of sock_wrapper, and will trigger to UAF.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This is similar to this issue: [



<span class="line"><!---->This is similar to this issue: [<!----></span>





https://bugs.chromium.org/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1233942](https://bugs.chromium.org/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1233942)



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://bugs.chromium.org/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1233942](https://bugs.chromium.org/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1233942)"><!---->https://bugs.chromium.org/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1233942](https://bugs.chromium.org/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1233942)<!----></a>



<br>



<br>

Sorry I missed the notification, and thanks 



<span class="line"><!---->Sorry I missed the notification, and thanks <!----></span>





eternalsakuraalpha@gmail.com



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="/u/eternalsakuraalpha@gmail.com"><!---->eternalsakuraalpha@gmail.com<!----></a>





 for filing the issue and the detailed analysis.



<span class="line"><!----> for filing the issue and the detailed analysis.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





 > Because the Android Client can actually disconnect the mojo at any time and OnBluetoothConnectingSocketReady runs in a separate thread in the thread pool



<span class="line"><!----> &gt; Because the Android Client can actually disconnect the mojo at any time and OnBluetoothConnectingSocketReady runs in a separate thread in the thread pool<!----></span>



<br>





I'm not sure about this assumption. I assume that the tasks involved in this issue should be scheduled by a sequenced scheduler, that is, they can be ran on different threads, but they will not be ran at the same time.



<span class="line"><!---->I'm not sure about this assumption. I assume that the tasks involved in this issue should be scheduled by a sequenced scheduler, that is, they can be ran on different threads, but they will not be ran at the same time.<!----></span>



<br>





So if CloseBluetoothConnectingSocket() is called at first, it will erase the socket wrapper, and since OnBluetoothConnectingSocketReady() is bound to the FileDescriptorWatcher::Controller inside that socket wrapper, when the socket wrapper is erased, the OnBluetoothConnectingSocketReady() task will also be cancelled if it is in the queue now, so it will not be executed.



<span class="line"><!---->So if CloseBluetoothConnectingSocket() is called at first, it will erase the socket wrapper, and since OnBluetoothConnectingSocketReady() is bound to the FileDescriptorWatcher::Controller inside that socket wrapper, when the socket wrapper is erased, the OnBluetoothConnectingSocketReady() task will also be cancelled if it is in the queue now, so it will not be executed.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





But I'm not too familiar with the task running model for ARC in Chrome, could hidehiko@ check if my understanding is correct? Thanks!



<span class="line"><!---->But I'm not too familiar with the task running model for ARC in Chrome, could hidehiko@ check if my understanding is correct? Thanks!<!----></span>

I had an offline chat with hidehiko@, and realized that I didn't read the reported issue correctly (sorry about that) and had a wrong understanding on that ThreadPool::PostTask() function...



<span class="line"><!---->I had an offline chat with hidehiko@, and realized that I didn't read the reported issue correctly (sorry about that) and had a wrong understanding on that ThreadPool::PostTask() function...<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Yes, the concern in #1 is valid. OnBluetoothConnectingSocketReady() posted with ThreadPool::PostTask() will be ran at a completely different task runner, so the issue could happen. I guess that I was confused because this is not the common code path, since we have a nonblocking socket, connect() on it should rarely return success directly (if it could happen), in most cases, the task posted by FileDescriptorWatcher below should be used, while this one is safe.



<span class="line"><!---->Yes, the concern in #1 is valid. OnBluetoothConnectingSocketReady() posted with ThreadPool::PostTask() will be ran at a completely different task runner, so the issue could happen. I guess that I was confused because this is not the common code path, since we have a nonblocking socket, connect() on it should rarely return success directly (if it could happen), in most cases, the task posted by FileDescriptorWatcher below should be used, while this one is safe.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Patch in #16 should have fixed this issue. Thanks for reporting this!



<span class="line"><!---->Patch in #16 should have fixed this issue. Thanks for reporting this!<!----></span>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.



<span class="line"><!---->Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.<!----></span>

        /*
         * Really specific class names are necessary because ShadowDOM
         * is disabled for this component.
         */
        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          color: var(--chops-link-color);
          position: absolute;
          background: var(--chops-white);
          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tbody {
          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr {
          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr[data-selected] {
          background: var(--chops-active-choice-bg);
          text-decoration: underline;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container td {
          padding: 0.25em 8px;
          white-space: nowrap;
        }
        .screenreader-hidden {
          clip: rect(1px, 1px, 1px, 1px);
          height: 1px;
          overflow: hidden;
          position: absolute;
          white-space: nowrap;
          width: 1px;
        }
